"

"diagnoses of drugs primarily affecting the autonomic nervous system\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of drugs primarily affecting the autonomic nervous system. drugs primarily affecting the autonomic nervous system is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code y51. icd-10 also has the following drugs primarily affecting the autonomic nervous system children in its four-character category: y51.0 (anticholinesterase agents); y51.1 (other parasympathomimetics [cholinergics]); y51.2 (ganglionic blocking drugs, not elsewhere classified); y51.3 (other parasympatholytics [anticholinergics and antimuscarinics] and spasmolytics, not elsewhere classified); y51.4 (predominantly alpha-adrenoreceptor agonists, not elsewhere classified); y51.5 (predominantly beta-adrenoreceptor agonists, not elsewhere classified); y51.6 (alpha-adrenoreceptor antagonists, not elsewhere classified); y51.7 (beta-adrenoreceptor antagonists, not elsewhere classified); y51.8 (centrally acting and adrenergic-neuron-blocking agents, not elsewhere classified); y51.9 (other and unspecified drugs primarily affecting the autonomic nervous system). . "

"diagnoses of other medical procedures as the cause of abnormal reaction of the patient, or of later complication, without mention of misadventure at the time of the procedure\u00a0\u00a0. in this classification, this covers the group of activities that yields a diagnosis of other medical procedures as the cause of abnormal reaction of the patient, or of later complication, without mention of misadventure at the time of the procedure. other medical procedures as the cause of abnormal reaction of the patient, or of later complication, without mention of misadventure at the time of the procedure is listed in the world health organizations international statistical classification of diseases and related health problems (icd-10) as a four-character category under code y84. icd-10 also has the following other medical procedures as the cause of abnormal reaction of the patient, or of later complication, without mention of misadventure at the time of the procedure children in its four-character category: y84.0 (cardiac catheterization); y84.1 (kidney dialysis); y84.2 (radiological procedure and radiotherapy); y84.3 (shock therapy); y84.4 (aspiration of fluid); y84.5 (insertion of gastric or duodenal sound); y84.6 (urinary catheterization); y84.7 (blood-sampling); y84.8 (other medical procedures); y84.9 (medical procedure, unspecified). . "
